China Merchants Bureau's Shanghai-Qingdao Route "Puan" Steamer Robbed by Pirates Outside Wusong Estuary, Fifteen Pirates Force Change of Course to Shanghai-Guangdong Route, Pirates Disembark at Zhao'an, Kidnapping Nine Passengers, Losses Approximately Five or Six Thousand Gold, Expected to Return to Shanghai Today

The China Merchants Bureau's "Puan" steamer, which departed from Shanghai to Qingdao on the 13th of this month, was robbed by fifteen pirates who boarded the ship in Shanghai disguised as passengers. The robbery occurred eighteen nautical miles north of Sheweishan Island outside the Wusong Estuary. The pirates forced the ship to sail towards the Shantou sea area. A large amount of silver, money, and goods were robbed. Before leaving, they kidnapped nine passengers. The Shanghai Bureau has telegraphed the Ministry of the Navy to dispatch warships to pursue and rescue the passengers, and ordered "Puan" to return to Shanghai. It is expected to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon. The details are as follows:

Heading to Qingdao

The "Puan" steamer was originally a transport warship of the Ministry of the Navy. Last year, it was leased to the China Merchants Bureau. It was initially used for the Putuo-Qingdao route. Due to its large size and spacious passenger cabins, and after major repairs by the China Merchants Bureau, it was well-received by passengers. After the lease expired last year, it was renewed for three months and converted to a dedicated Shanghai-Qingdao route, focusing on passenger transport. On the 13th of this month, it departed from Shanghai to Qingdao with more than fifty first, second, and third-class passengers and over 11,000 pieces of cargo. The journey from Shanghai to Qingdao usually takes 28 hours and it was scheduled to arrive in Qingdao at 2:00 PM on the 14th. However, it did not arrive on time. The director of the Qingdao branch was in Shanghai on official business and instructed an employee to send a telegram to the Shanghai headquarters to inquire. The Shanghai headquarters received the report and initially suspected that there was fog on the sea and that "Puan" might be anchored en route. It ordered the wireless station operator Fang Ziwei to send a telegram with the call sign XNPA, but there was no response. They were very anxious. Yesterday, they received a telegram from Qingdao stating that crew members of the Yisheng steamer of Jardine Matheson & Co., which was heading to Qingdao, reported seeing "Puan" off course and heading south, causing even greater concern. It was not until 9:00 PM last night that they received a telegram from the ship owner of "Puan" reporting the robbery.

Pirates Mix In

When "Puan" departed from Shanghai, it was docked at the Hua Zhan pier in Pudong. The ship was scheduled to depart at 9:30 AM on Saturday, but on the 13th, it was delayed until 10:15 AM. At that time, first and second-class passengers had already boarded the ship. Just as the ship was about to set sail, more than ten third-class passengers rushed to board and also boarded "Puan" to Qingdao. The crew members were busy with departure preparations and did not pay attention to these passengers. According to Sheng Wunian, the comprador of another steamer, who was unharmed, he was disembarking from "Puan" when it was untied and saw this group of passengers boarding the ship just before departure. Their actions seemed suspicious, but the ship had already started moving and it was inconvenient to inspect them again. The ship's personnel did not suspect that pirates had mixed in. By the time "Puan" cleared customs, the matter had passed. It was only when the news of the robbery reached Shanghai that it was realized that the pirates had planned carefully, fearing that they would be discovered if they boarded the ship too early. Therefore, they waited until departure to board, taking advantage of the timing to sneak onto the ship.

Control the Whole Ship

The fifteen pirates, all speaking Cantonese, had weapons hidden on their bodies and were scattered throughout the third-class cabins. Since the ship had no iron railings or anti-theft measures, all levels of cabins, the bridge, and the pilot's platform were freely accessible. According to the ship owner's subsequent telegram, "Puan" had left the Wusong Estuary and traveled eighteen nautical miles north of Sheweishan Island, and was sailing north. The pirates then emerged from the third-class cabins, each holding a pistol. They fired shots as a signal and rushed to the ship owner's room, first forcing the ship owner, Rex, and the first and second officers to be under surveillance. They also occupied the wireless room, took the telegraph operator Zhu Shun into custody, and prohibited communication. At this time, there was no naval escort on the ship. The ship owner and others were forced to hand over their self-defense pistols. The crew members lost the ability to resist and had to adopt a policy of non-resistance. The entire ship was under the control of the pirates, who forced the ship owner to order a change of direction and head towards the Shantou sea area. This occurred after 4:00 PM on the 13th.

Robbery Situation

After taking control of the entire ship, the pirates began to rob. They first searched the main dining room and the second-class cabins, then proceeded to rob the third-class cabins. All cash, silver dollars, banknotes, and women's jewelry carried by the passengers were robbed. Finally, the better clothes and items carried by the passengers were also robbed. After several rounds of looting, everything owned by the passengers and crew was completely looted. The stolen goods were piled up in the cabins, and then the passengers' suitcases were taken to pack the loot. It is said that the silver dollars from ship tickets sold by the purser Zou Lun were also robbed. The total loss of cash, clothing, and other items is estimated at five or six thousand gold, but the exact amount will not be known until the ship arrives today.

Damage to Goods

The "Puan" ship was carrying 8,000 bags of flour, 113 bags of white rice, 15 pieces of foreign cloth, 2,187 pieces of paper, 124 boxes of cigarettes, 166 boxes of books, 211 barrels of oranges, and other items such as seafood, burlap sacks, and ironware, totaling more than 11,000 pieces. However, there were no valuable goods. The pirates forced the crew to open the cargo hold and take out a box of cigarettes, which they opened and smoked freely, distributing them to the passengers. They also opened a piece of foreign cloth and took out several bolts to use for hoisting stolen goods for escape at sea. The remaining goods were not touched, so the loss of goods was minimal.

Nine Passengers Kidnapped

After looting, the pirates expressed disappointment at the meager gains. They then kidnapped passengers from the cabins. Among the passengers on the "Puan," there were sixteen first and second-class passengers, including four women and four children, and more than forty third-class passengers. The pirates kidnapped nine male passengers from the first and second-class cabins but did not disturb the women and children. The names of the kidnapped passengers (the China Merchants Bureau has a list that can be checked, so they are omitted). Sun Zhenwu, the director of the Qingdao branch of the China Merchants Bureau, happened to be returning to Qingdao on "Puan." Upon hearing the news of the robbery, he disguised himself as a sailor and managed to escape being kidnapped. The purser Zou Lun and the crew were not kidnapped.

Fishing Boat Transports Loot

Around 7:00 PM on the 15th, the "Puan" steamer had sailed to the Zhao'an sea area at the intersection of Fujian and Guangdong provinces. After completing the robbery, several pirates searched along the coast and found two fishing boats. They forced "Puan" to stop and transferred the stolen goods and the nine kidnapped passengers to the fishing boats in the Zhao'an sea area and left. After the pirates left the ship, the ship owner and others began to organize everything, determine the navigation route, and sail to Shantou for temporary mooring. They telegraphed the Shanghai headquarters to report the robbery.

Telegrams to Apprehend Pirates

The first telegram from "Puan" reporting the robbery arrived in Shanghai at 9:00 PM on the 15th. Since no one was in the office, it was sent to Liu Hongsheng. At 11:30 PM, they received a second telegram from the ship owner. Liu Hongsheng, together with the Shipping Department, began planning to apprehend the pirates and rescue the kidnapped passengers. At midnight, they sent a telegram to the Ministry of the Navy, stating: "According to the ship owner of 'Puan', on the first day of the month, the ship arrived eighteen nautical miles north of Sheweishan Island, and pirates disguised as passengers robbed the passengers, who were all looted. Before leaving, the pirates kidnapped nine passengers. Please quickly telegraph the fleet stationed in Fujian to pursue and rescue the kidnapped passengers. Liu Hongsheng of the state-run China Merchants Bureau." After sending this telegram, they also sent telegrams to the branches in Shantou, Xiamen, and Fujian, instructing them to request local army and police assistance in the pursuit to prevent the pirates from escaping far.

Ship Already Sailing Back

Yesterday, Liu Hongsheng sent a wireless telegram to the ship owner of "Puan", ordering the ship to return to Shanghai from Shantou immediately. Yesterday afternoon, they received a telegram from "Puan" stating that it had already set sail and was en route, estimated to be heading north at 25 degrees 37 minutes north latitude and 120 degrees east longitude. However, due to severe weather, it is expected to arrive in Shanghai this afternoon or tomorrow morning.

Inquiries from All Parties

After this incident occurred yesterday, many family members of passengers who had boarded the ship went to the China Merchants Bureau to inquire about the situation. The General Affairs Department of the Bureau provided answers and comforted them, stating that they had requested the Navy authorities to rescue them. Yesterday, Liu Hongsheng also submitted a report to the Ministry on the "Puan" robbery based on the ship owner's report. The ship's losses were minor, and the crew members were not injured.

To Host Banquet for Nanjing Authorities Today

British Aviation Commissioner Mr. Willock Arrives in Shanghai

Says China Needs a Large Quantity of British Aircraft

According to the *Continental Daily News*, Captain Willock, the aviation commissioner of the British Embassy in China, who was dispatched by the British government in September last year at the request of the then British Ambassador to China, Sir Miles Lampson, arrived in Shanghai on the mail ship *Rampurla* on Sunday. He is currently staying at the Cathay Hotel and will go to Beijing within a few days and then to Shanghai to set up an office. This is Mr. Willock's first visit to China. He told a reporter from the *Continental Daily News* that he had just unpacked his luggage and could not yet discuss or express his plans or opinions on China's aviation industry. However, he dared to say that China needs an unlimited number of various types of British aircraft, so he will pay close attention to the great progress of China's military and civilian aviation industry in the future. It is reported that Captain Willock served in the Light Infantry during the European War and transferred to the Royal Flying Corps in 1915, where he repeatedly achieved meritorious service. After the end of the European War, he worked in the Air Ministry and was involved with the British Air Defense Committee.

Sino-British Communication Test Completed, Opening Ceremony Decided for Early Next Month

The Public Will be Invited to Visit at That Time

According to the Central News Agency, the Zhenru Sino-British Wireless Radio Station of the International Telecommunications Bureau of the Ministry of Communications has been conducting communication tests since the 12th. In order to understand the current status of the Sino-British communication test and the opening date of the station, a reporter from the Central News Agency specially visited Director Lu of the Bureau yesterday. According to him,

Excellent Test Results

The wireless transmitter for Sino-British communication is a high-power shortwave spark gap wireless transmitter, which was ordered from the British Marconi Wireless Telegraph Company. It is the latest type of equipment. The tests have been excellent since 3:00 PM on the 12th. The tests are still in progress because the test work requires testing each item one by one, and the work is very complex. It is expected to be completed by the end of this week.

The Public Will be Invited Soon

Wen Yuqing, Director of the International Telecommunications Bureau, has decided to hold an opening ceremony in Zhenru after the completion of the test work. At that time, Zhu Jiaji, Minister of Communications, will attend the grand ceremony. The opening date is scheduled for early next month. If the test work is very smooth, it is planned to open on the 3rd of next month. If there is not enough time, it will be postponed to the 10th of next month. It has also been decided to invite the press and all sectors of society the day before the opening to report on the preparation process. In order to make everything clear to all sectors of society, Mr. Wen has already compiled a report booklet, which details the functions of the station, the construction costs, and equipment diagrams, so that it can be distributed to guests at that time.

Sino-US Test Report Inaccurate

Director Lu believes that the report in yesterday's newspapers that the station will hold a Sino-US test report after the completion of the Sino-British test report is inaccurate. He also said that China and the United States have already formally communicated and there is no need for a test report. Moreover, the equipment for Sino-British communication is spark gap shortwave, which can only be used for communication between China and the United Kingdom and cannot be used for communication with the United States. As for the prices after Sino-British communication, they are the same as the prices set by foreign companies.

Various Organizations' Rent Reduction Movement Held a Delegates' Assembly Yesterday, Resolved to Organize Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, Zhang Yichen, Wang Hanliang, and 33 Others as Members, Issued Declaration, Passed Committee's Organizational Regulations

Various organizations in this city, in view of the economic depression and commercial decline, in order to demand a reduction in rent to ease the burden and maintain livelihood, specially held a delegates' assembly of various organizations in this city at 2:00 PM yesterday in the hall of the City Chamber of Commerce at Tianhougong Bridge. More than 100 delegates attended the meeting, resolved to organize the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Movement Committee, and issued a declaration. The details are as follows:

Attending Delegates

The attendees yesterday included Zhang Yichen, Hu Fengxiang, Cao Zhigong from the First Special District Citizens' Federation, Huang Xianggu from the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Huang Songshan from the Shoe Nail Industry, Huang **from the Gauze Flower, Gu Linshi from the Flower Tree Industry, Zou Yuqing and Song Tiren from the Fenjiu Wine Industry, Jiang **qing and He Xitang from the Copper Bar and Old Iron Guild, Jin Chuxiang from the Salted Fish Industry, Sun Choucheng from the New** Guild, Sun Fuji from the National Products Factory Federation, Cheng Weisheng from the Silk Industry, Wang Hanqiang from the National Products Maintenance Association, Luo Hanzhang from the Shoe Industry Guild, Zhu Wanzhang from the Inland River Shipping Industry, Yao Zhaoji from the Travel Industry, Ren Nongxuan from Traditional Medicine, Ding Minqiang and Hu Songsheng from the Cotton Industry, Zhang Lishen from the Steamboat Timber Industry, Xue Guangqian from the University Federation, Wang Honghui from the Chemical Raw Materials Industry Guild, Ge Futian from the Nantong Native Place Association, and Tu Kaizheng, Liu Zhongying, Zhu Yangwo, Shu Huizhen, Zhang Xianfang, Ma Junshuo from the Citizens' District Branches, and representatives from various other organizations, approximately more than 100 people.

Meeting Circumstances

After performing the rituals, Wang Hanliang, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Yichen, Xue Guangqian, Ye Jiaxing, Huang Xianggu, and Cao Zhigong were publicly elected as the presidium, Yuan Hongjun as the master of ceremonies, and Zhu Yangwu, Xu Letian, and Zheng Dongshan as the recorders. First, Chairman Cao Zhigong reported the purpose of the meeting, and then began to discuss the proposals from various parties, resolved to organize the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, and appointed 35 people, including Zhang Yichen, as members. The meeting adjourned around 5:00 PM.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Cao Zhigong's report stated briefly: The reason for convening the delegates' assembly of various organizations today is that after the January 28th Incident, the city's situation has been deteriorating day by day, but rents in various places have not only not been reduced, but in many places they are still being increased. Although the Nanjing area is prosperous, there are many empty houses. Under the abnormal circumstances of expensive rents and a declining market, the city's citizens can no longer bear the burden. It is necessary to find a way to remedy the situation. In view of this, the First Special District Citizens' Federation has specially convened the delegates' assembly of various organizations to discuss together and hopes that the delegates will express their opinions to promote progress.

Important Resolutions

The following cases were discussed yesterday: (1) Declaration case, (resolved) passed; (2) Organization of the committee case, (resolved) A. passed the organizational outline, B. the presidium appointed Cao Zhigong, Sun Mingqi, Zhu Yangwu, Wang Fenghui, Huang Xianggu, etc. as members of the nomination committee, C. the nomination committee submitted a report and the members were elected by the entire meeting; (3) Draft rent reduction principles, A. the reduction principles were submitted to the committee for detailed discussion, B. if various circles have opinions, please submit them in writing and submit them to the committee for discussion together; (4) Illegal abolition of the lunar calendar rent collection should be cancelled, (resolved) passed; (5) Property tax should still be paid according to the original amount, (resolved) passed; (6) A letter from a tenant on Taihe Street requesting that Chinese people be pro-foreign and that foreign lawyers should be restricted from renting, (resolved) send a letter to the Younigan lawyer; (7) The old landlord transfers the household to the new landlord, and rent should not be increased, (resolved) passed; (8) The rent of new houses should not exceed the original rent of old houses, (resolved) passed; (9) Secret; (10) The Silk Industry Guild proposed four rent reduction methods, (resolved) A. principle passed, B. submitted to the committee for discussion; (11) How to raise the funds of this association, (resolved) to set five yuan, ten yuan, and thirty yuan, and various organizations should bear the amount according to their ability.

List of Members

The list of members of the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, designated by the nomination committee and passed by all the delegates, is as follows: Ye Jiaxing, Zhang Yichen, Xue Guangqian, Wang Hanliang, Hu Fengxiang, Zhu Xuefan, Yuan Hongjun, Cao Zhigong, Chen Binghui, Liu Zhongying, Mao Ruyuan, Cheng Yujie, Sun Mingqi, Jin Chuxiang, Wang Hesong, Zhu Yangwu, Zhang Dafu, Zhang Xianfang, Gu Wensheng, Wang Honghui, Chen Jiufeng, Huang Xianggu, Mao Yun, Wang Manyun, He Yuanming, Chen Jicheng, Xie Zhongfu, Gao Junshuo, Shao Xubai, Zhu Zhichun, Zhou Funong, Hong Songjiong, Shu Huizhen, Cai Qiajun, Li Ruzhang, etc., 35 people as members, and Ye Jiaxing, Wang Hanliang, and Zhang Yichen were appointed as conveners.

Organizational Regulations

The organizational regulations of the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, Article 1, this association is named the Shanghai Municipal Rent Reduction Committee, Article 2, the purpose of this association is to reduce the burden of rent and restore the prosperity of the market, Article 3, this association shall have 35 executive committee members, who shall be elected and organized by the delegates' assembly of various organizations, and nine standing committee members shall be mutually elected by the executive committee members to handle daily affairs, Article 4, this association shall have five departments: general affairs, investigation, organization, finance, and publicity, and each department shall have a director and deputy director, who shall be mutually elected by the executive committee members, Article 5, this association may establish special committees as needed in fact, and invite people with reputation from all walks of life to serve as them, and may consider administrative personnel to assist the progress of the association's affairs, Article 6, the executive committee shall meet once every two weeks, and the standing committee shall meet once a week, and the director and deputy director of each department may attend, Article 7, the delegates' assembly of this association has no fixed date and shall be convened at any time by the executive committee, Article 8, the expenses of this association shall be borne by various organizations, Article 9, these regulations shall be implemented after being passed by the delegates' assembly of various organizations, and the same shall apply to its amendments.

Declaration

Shanghai is our country's premier commercial port, a vital hub for land and water transportation, and a center where merchants gather, and talent and wealth mostly congregate. The city's population has already reached over three million, accounting for more than five percent of the entire populations of countries like Italy and Japan. It leads in trends, its culture is rapidly advancing, and its industry and commerce are increasingly prosperous. It has subtly taken the lead in guiding the interior. We, the citizens of Shanghai, can certainly boast of this, but we should also know how to motivate ourselves. If we can rely on the innate intelligence of the great Chinese nation, strive with unity, and diligently manage our affairs, then not only will we prosper our city, but we will also advance all our fellow countrymen to a realm of wealth and strength. This should not be too difficult. However, in recent years, the market has shown signs of decline, all industries show signs of decay, foreign goods are increasingly flooding in, and unemployment is increasing daily, to the point where everyone is just trying to get by. This has turned into a makeshift situation. Alas, society has declined to such an extent! What is the reason for this? Although there are various reasons, the biggest key is the gift of the January 28th Incident. At that time, the Japanese army did everything possible to bombard the Zhabei area with artillery fire for more than fifty consecutive days. All commercial and civilian storage areas were reduced to ashes, and areas with connected Chinese houses were turned into ruins. Even the distant Nanshi and Pudong were left with neither homes nor markets. Although there were foreigners living in the concessions, their situation was different, and the impact was still alarming. Electric wires were tangled in the middle of the roads, airplanes came to drop bombs from time to time, rumors spread, and there were several scares in one night. Merchants hoarded goods at high prices, and refugees surged like tides. Factories and shops were forced to close, and even more staff and workers lost their jobs. Some were separated from their wives and children, and some committed suicide by jumping into the river. All kinds of tragedies emerged endlessly. The visible and expressible losses were countless, and the hidden and unacknowledged losses were definitely hundreds or thousands of times greater. This means absorbing intangible losses and being indirectly burdened by intangible losses. The entire city suffered such a huge and unique wound, and the unlimited losses made the situation at the time unbearable. The aftermath was even more difficult to arrange. In addition, current life and production are even more difficult. If vitality is not restored one day, society will not be stable one day. Although the war is two years past, the city's situation has not improved. This is a matter of trying to make ends meet, and the facts make it so. I believe that there are many ways to revive this city, but to replenish the foundation and cultivate the root, we must choose the most urgent, closest, and most common matter of reducing housing rents. This definitely needs to be resolved immediately. This is because the problem of housing for people is more important than clothing and food. Clothing and food are certainly related to being cold and hungry, but there are still ways to settle them. Housing is related to life and death, and it is a real need. Not only can it shelter from wind, frost, rain, and snow, and accommodate food, lodging, and storage, but also family life, birth, old age, sickness, death, marriage, sacrifices, and even the interactions of relatives and friends, and the arrangement of work all require housing. Therefore, the housing problem has also become important. Shanghai's rents are the highest in the country. The social environment has never been as pressing as it is today. If tenants can maintain their livelihood, who would want to cause trouble? Who would have known that at this time when vitality has not recovered and the city's situation is declining, there are a few capitalists and real estate operators who disregard the people's livelihood and only know their own interests, repeatedly raising rents to make up for their losses in old age. Houses that cost only ten or more yuan a month a few years ago now cost dozens of yuan. It is difficult to satisfy their greed by raising rents, so houses can be renovated. This has become a common practice, and society does not pay attention to it and allows it to happen naturally. As a result, all tenants find it difficult to afford it, resentment arises, and public opinion boils. Most of the blood and sweat of a family or shop is transferred to the landlord. Other necessary expenses, no matter how urgent, are only allowed to be delayed. Sometimes, if payment is delayed, in addition to the unreasonable actions of the real estate agency, lawyer letters and court summonses come one after another, and there is almost no peace. If they leave the house in anger, it is impossible to do so. If they listen to the exploitation, it is difficult to cope with. They cannot live in peace or enjoy their work. The reality is like this, and the future is bleak. It is not just the end of one family or one shop, but the same end for all families and shops in the city. Because they cannot survive, those who come from the poor areas of the interior to obtain the qualifications of Shanghai tenants are even more at an end. However, when the January 28th Incident ended, some areas of the city close to the war zone were exempted from rent for three or four months or one or two months. However, this can only be regarded as a temporary emergency measure, and absolutely cannot be regarded as enough to make amends. The Principle of People's Livelihood advocated by the late Premier Sun Yat-sen is intended to ensure the necessities of our people's lives. Today's Shanghai landlords are acting against the tide, ignoring the people's suffering. Are they not too heartless? However, there are differences among them. Some are ignorant of the general trend, some have their power taken by flatterers, and some dare not reduce rents alone. We should not regard them as all the same. In recent days, there are often empty houses in the busy city, and there are frequent disputes over rent collection. Even rent advertisements often have new rules for reducing rent by a certain amount and giving one month's rent. This further proves the unreliability of one party's exploitation and the exhaustion of the other party's ability. Alas, the city's situation is declining year by year, and we are still worried about not having a way to remedy it. How can we impose more shackles? We live here, how can we sit idly by and watch society collapse and decline without providing assistance? The matter is urgent, and the situation is pressing. Our association is duty-bound and cannot refuse to participate in this rent reduction movement for the sake of solving the people's difficulties in Suzhou, for the sake of ensuring social tranquility, for the sake of restoring vitality, and for the sake of revitalizing the market. Most of the landlords are Chinese, and money can communicate with the gods, and society should be maintained. Once the tide has turned, how can we survive? If the market recovers, there will be no future worries. Rather than expecting the impossible, why not make small profits for a long time? Even foreigners advocate co-existence and co-prosperity, how can Chinese abandon themselves? If they can suddenly realize this and immediately and voluntarily reduce their rents, then not only will the tenants be grateful, but the entire society will also benefit greatly. This matter is of great importance and depends on the collective wisdom and efforts of everyone. Our countrymen and leaders will definitely sympathize with us. Therefore, we make this declaration, hoping that you will consider it carefully.

Special Commissioner of the Ministry of Finance's Document to President Wang Regarding the Kim Seok Case: In Fact, There is No Dispute Over Kim's Nationality, and Even According to Japanese Law, There is No Need to Explicitly Allow it

Yesterday, Lou Yunmei, the representative lawyer for Kim Seok, submitted a document to President Wang, which read: "To President Wang, with utmost respect, regarding the case of Kim Seok's illegal arrest by the Japanese Consul, the detailed facts and negotiation process have been submitted in a special document, and I believe that you have reviewed them. However, I recently received a letter from Mr. Zhi, stating that you said, 'The difficulty lies in that Kim Seok himself admits that he has obtained Chinese nationality, while the Japanese side does not recognize Kim Seok's renunciation of Japanese nationality as valid. The future nationality of the two countries is the most contentious issue between China and Japan regarding Koreans.' His judgment is correct, and his observation is insightful, and it is difficult to find anyone who could surpass it. However, based on the facts of this case, there should be no dispute over Kim Seok's nationality. Furthermore, according to legal principles, regardless of whether Kim Seok has renounced Japanese nationality or not, and residing within Chinese territory, there is no doubt that Kim Seok should be subject to Chinese law. In order to clarify the truth and facilitate negotiations, the facts and laws are presented in detail as follows:"

Facts

"Kim Seok has been setting up residence in Shanghai, China for six consecutive years since October of the 18th year of the Republic of China, when he naturalized in China with his father. This alone is sufficient to prove the fact that he is a Chinese citizen. Furthermore, Kim Seok and his father were arrested in the same way last November. At that time, our government, based on Kim Seok's certificate of nationality, seriously negotiated with the Japanese side, which finally agreed to release him. If the Japanese side did not recognize Kim Seok's renunciation of his nationality and his naturalization in China, why did it not raise the dispute over nationality at that time and refuse to release him? It was not until now that it re-issued this fallacy. I really do not understand its intentions. Therefore, based on the facts, Kim Seok's nationality issue has been determined once, and it cannot be allowed to be disputed again, undermining our sovereignty."

Legal Aspects

"Based on the above facts, regardless of whether the Japanese side has tacitly approved Kim Seok's naturalization in China, according to Article 20, Paragraph 1 of the Japanese Nationality Law, 'A person who acquires a foreign nationality voluntarily loses Japanese nationality.' There is no need for explicit approval from the Japanese government, and there are no special provisions for Koreans to renounce their nationality. Japan adopts a purely laissez-faire policy towards its citizens renouncing their nationality. From the perspective of Chinese law, there is only Chinese nationality. According to the general principles of international law, this is a natural conclusion. Even if we take a step back, even if Kim Seok has not lost his Japanese nationality because he has not been approved by the Japanese government, Kim Seok has already legally obtained Chinese nationality. At most, he can only be considered to have obtained dual nationality. According to the Nationality Law Convention signed by various countries in The Hague in 1934, Article 5 stipulates that 'Within the territory of a third country, a person with more than one nationality shall be deemed to have only one nationality. Without prejudice to the application of the law of that country to matters of personal status and to the validity of treaties, that country shall, of all the nationalities of that person, choose the nationality of the country where his habitual or principal residence is situated, or, in other circumstances, the nationality of the country which appears to be most closely connected with him, and recognize it as his sole nationality.' Now that Kim Seok has naturalized in China and his family has lived in Shanghai for six years, the country with which he has the closest relationship should naturally be recognized as China. Even if Kim Seok lived in France, it should be handled in this way, let alone living in China. According to the interpretation of the above-mentioned legal text, this is a natural conclusion. Moreover, the fact that Kim Seok is a Chinese citizen has been proven by facts and the tacit approval of the Japanese side. Therefore, according to the region where he resides, the Second Special District of Shanghai, it should naturally be handled in accordance with the agreement on the establishment of Chinese courts in the French Concession of Shanghai. However, they are actually breaking the agreement heartlessly. Therefore, China's regret to the French Consulate is no less than that to the Japanese Consulate. Based on the above explanations, there is no doubt that Kim Seok should be a Chinese citizen, according to the facts and the law. I respectfully request you to review and approve it, and promptly lodge a serious protest and negotiation with the French and Japanese consulates to release him, so as to protect our sovereignty. I respectfully submit this, and wish you peace and tranquility. Lawyer Lou Yunmei"

The Shanghai Northern Rice Industry Porters Petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday

Demanding an Immediate Solution and Waiting Until Late Without Dispersing

The Joint Rice Industry Conference Unanimously and Firmly Refused

"The Shanghai Northern Rice Industry porter labor dispute, since the new and old workers had a dispute the day before yesterday, the porters petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau yesterday, and the rice industry held a meeting to discuss countermeasures, deciding to refuse porter labor, otherwise they would rather stop work altogether to deal with it. The details are as follows:"

Porters' Petition

"Shi Dengfu, the foreman of the Hongtai Yuji Porter Company, and all the workers, because they had a business license, had repeatedly fought for work. After a dispute with the dock workers the day before yesterday, yesterday morning at 10 o'clock, Shi Dengfu, Wang Dafu, Yang Zhenrun, and others led more than 120 workers, wearing red vests, from Wuzhen Road Bridge to the city center to petition the Social Affairs Bureau, demanding that the third item of the previous commercial solution be implemented, ordering all factories to settle them. They arrived at about 1 p.m., and were received by Wang Gang, a staff member of the Third Section. He said that regarding the issue of settling unemployed workers, the bureau had ordered the submission of a list of names, but the lists submitted repeatedly were inconsistent and varied greatly, making them unreliable. Now that the workers had come to the bureau to petition, he immediately registered them. As a result, only more than 80 of the 120 workers were on the previous list, and the rest could not be checked. Wang then advised the visitors, saying that after the bureau verified that the workers were indeed former porters, it would order all factories to settle them. Most of the workers were satisfied and gradually dispersed. However, a small number of workers, about 40, demanded an immediate solution and waited without leaving. After Wang repeatedly persuaded them, they became unreasonable, and he had no choice but to send the police to the scene to suppress them. As of 8 p.m., the workers were still lingering and had not dispersed."

Joint Rice Industry Conference

"The various rice industry groups in the city, because Shi Dengfu repeatedly led crowds to cause trouble, greatly affecting business, held a joint meeting at Cuixiu Hall yesterday afternoon at 4 o'clock. Representatives from the bean and rice industry guild, the rice milling industry guild, the Shanghai Southern and Shanghai Northern offices of the bean and rice industry, the Shanghai Southern and Shanghai Northern rice transport merchant association, and various firms, including Zhu Zixiang, Jiang Zisheng, Zhang Songtao, and others, totaling more than 70 people, attended. Zhu Zixiang chaired the meeting. First, the chairman and Jiang Zisheng reported the events of the disturbance the day before yesterday. After discussion, they all said that the foremen of each firm had guarantees and bore heavy responsibilities. They unanimously refused the Hongtai porters. If they still wanted to gather crowds to cause trouble, they would rather stop work throughout the city to deal with it. At the same time, they also petitioned the party and government to stop them. The meeting adjourned at 6 o'clock."

After the Founding Meeting of the China National Products Sales Company

Solemn Congratulations from Mayor Shi of Beijing

Encouraging People to Work Hard in Production

Helping the Government Build National Strength

"The China National Products Sales Joint Company held its founding meeting on the 15th of this month at the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. The details of the meeting were reported in yesterday's newspaper. The details of what we have obtained are continued as follows:"

British Love of National Products

"Mayor Shi of Nanjing City once studied in Britain, Belgium, France, and other countries, and stayed in Britain the longest. Therefore, he has a deep understanding of British politics and human affairs. This time, he represented the Beijing Municipal Government to attend the Shanghai meeting, wanting to express the spirit of cooperation between the government and the people, and wanting to introduce the human construction of British politics. On the same day, after being introduced by Chairman Wang Xiaolai, he stood up and gave a speech amidst applause from the entire audience. He said, 'I (referring to himself as the Mayor) came to Shanghai this time to celebrate the completion of the founding meeting of the China National Products Sales Joint Company. The organization of the China National Products Sales Joint Company is different from ordinary companies. The declaration calls it a bulwark of economic self-defense, which is its value. When the company was founded, I accepted the invitation of Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Wu Zhihao, and others, even though I knew that my ability was shallow. However, in view of the internal and external troubles, the disasters caused by nature and man, and the panic of social economy and rural bankruptcy, I really could not but do my best to follow suit. Today's China is like a dangerous boat drifting in stormy waves. The government and the people must work together in the same boat to save it. The plan adopted by the China National Products Sales Joint Company is far-reaching. I met with the author of the plan, Mr. Ren Jinpin, in Beijing. Mr. Ren called the company an organization against the East India Company and the South Manchuria Railway Company. If all the shareholders of the company and all the officials and people who care about it can support it, it will indeed be a great undertaking to save the country. The British political spirit is worthy of reference. During the European War, I happened to be in Britain, and the Anglo-Japanese alliance had not yet expired. However, British students secretly boycotted the Japanese goods sold in Britain. I was surprised and asked them, 'Our England is a country that implements commercial policies. If the people cannot compete to buy and love the country's goods, then the industrialists and merchants will be in starvation.' Looking at British history, we can see that it has fought more than 70 times for the right to sea transport and trade. From this, we can see the power of the British to exercise policy and build the psychology, and we can also see the source of British hegemony. The China National Products Sales Joint Company is an agency for the people to assist the government in implementing production policies. Therefore, I hope that after the company is established, it can do its best to assist both production and sales in accordance with the declaration and plan, jointly cooperate, and jointly seek production, so as to build the national strength as the foundation for the government to defend itself and resist foreign aggression.'

List of Elected Directors and Supervisors

"The election of directors and supervisors began at 6 p.m. the night before and the results were announced at about 9 p.m. A total of 21 directors were elected, including Kong Yongzhi, Du Yuesheng, Xu Jingren, Shi Liangcai, Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Chen Guangfu, Lang Zhihao, Zhou Zuomin, Shi Ying, Yu Qiaqing, Wu Tingsheng, Yu Zuoting, Zhou Guanhong, Hu Wenhu, Xue Chunsheng, Wang Boyuan, Xu Caicheng, Wang Yintai, Zhang Rongchu, and Xiang Weichen. Five supervisors were elected, including Xu Xinliu, Chen Gongbo, Fu Pinggui, Xiang Shengwu, and Zhang Shiqi. The shareholders present were all happy, believing that the reputation, knowledge, and ability of the elected directors and supervisors were sufficient to bear the heavy responsibility of the company and could fulfill the expectations of the shareholders and all sectors of society to implement the plan."

Mayor Shi Has Returned to Beijing

"After the founding meeting was completed, Mayor Shi returned to his residence in East Asia, packed his luggage, and was escorted by Ren Jinpin and Wu Guangzhi to the North Station at about 11 p.m., where he took the 12 o'clock train back to Beijing. The Mayor's trip to Shanghai was only to attend the founding meeting and had no other tasks."

Important Bills Passed

"In addition to amending the articles of association, the founding meeting also discussed and determined the capital, reporting that the total amount of shares was 260,500 yuan, which exceeded the stipulated amount of half of the required capital by 10,500 yuan. It was then resolved that the capital would first be registered with the Ministry of Industry at a total amount of 250,000 yuan, and then the board of directors would determine the method to continue to raise 250,000 yuan. The remaining 10,500 yuan would be discussed by the shareholders with larger investments to be set aside or recovered."

Women's National Products Propaganda Conference to Be Held at the City Chamber of Commerce This Afternoon, Many Celebrities from All Walks of Life Invited to Participate in Speeches, and High-Class Entertainment and Gifts to Add to the Fun

The details are divided as follows:"

Venue Layout

"The association borrowed the City Chamber of Commerce Hall at Tianhou Palace as the venue for the conference. A white cloth sign reading 'Shanghai First Special District Citizens' Union, Women's National Products Sports Propaganda Conference' was hung at the entrance. Declaration

The Women's National Products Movement Propaganda Conference of the First Special District Citizens' Association of this city issued a declaration stating that under the government's policy of preventing economic aggression by foreign powers in recent years, and in the autumn of the people's continuous promotion of the national products movement, the number of excess imports in foreign trade has increased since 1927. In the previous year, it even reached a huge sum of 900 million yuan. Last year was the National Products Year, and the number of excess imports should have decreased significantly. However, the fact is not so. The countryside is declining, and domestic goods are falling in price, while large quantities of cotton and wheat are purchased, resulting in an excess import of 800 million yuan. Fortunately, the purchasing power of the inland people has declined; otherwise, it would definitely exceed the number of 1932. Alas, how lamentable! Some Chinese people have a mentality that this is all the government's business, and the people are not involved. After several studies, we feel that this mentality is indeed wrong. If the people do not strive for self-improvement, it is difficult to blame the government, which is generated by the accumulation of the people, for being omnipotent. We believe that purchasing and using national products is a basic national obligation. However, some people, especially those in commercial ports with a foreign atmosphere, believe that national products are not as cheap and good as foreign goods, and they have various excuses and calculations, refusing to buy or use national products unless they are foreign goods. Then, the rulers will naturally be more concerned and serious about the country's affairs in many aspects. Moreover, individuals purchase and use national products as needed, and will not necessarily go bankrupt, while a slight impatience with the country's affairs will lead to immediate destruction. This is truly the epitome of being harsh on others and lenient on oneself. Last year was designated as "National Products Year," but it did not have a significant effect on the development of national products. This year, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the Shanghai Municipal Association, and various women's organizations have jointly designated this year as the "Women's National Products Year." Women's patriotism is purer than that of men. A certain lawyer once showed no sympathy for patriotic people and even attacked them severely, but his wife forced him to change his ways. From this, it can be seen that the effectiveness of women purchasing and using national products will definitely surpass that of men. Since last year's National Products Year, our association has been constantly calling out after being initiated by various leading groups. We dare not make an exception for this year's Women's National Products Year. Therefore, at 1:00 p.m. on January 17th, we will hold a propaganda conference at the auditorium of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, hoping to save the country by saving ourselves, starting from the family, and starting from women. The beginning of saving the country is to purchase and use national products, for women to purchase and use national products, and for women who control the family to purchase and use national products.

The Wuding Road Police Station Cracks Down on Red Pill Manufacturing

Confiscates Poisonous Substances and Detains Four People

Mastermind Jiang Peisheng Has Escaped

Sun Aizhong, the chief inspector of the General Police Station, received a report from an informant the day before yesterday, stating that someone was privately setting up a red pill manufacturing facility at No. 10 Wuding Village, Wuding Road, producing a large number of pills every day and distributing them to various brothels. He reported this to Inspector Lu Liankui and Western Inspector Bai Pu, and specially requested the First Special District Court to issue a search warrant. Yesterday afternoon, at around 4:00 p.m., he assisted Chinese Inspectors Feng Zhiming and Song Bingzheng in secretly conducting a search. When they arrived at the room upstairs, they saw that red pills were being manufactured. They confiscated six and a half pounds of red pills, another four bags totaling two pounds, as well as a complete set of red pill manufacturing equipment, two pounds of rock sugar, two cans of pigment powder, scales, suitcases, and other items. They detained four people, including Pan Huizhong, Huai Axing, Zhou Huiwen, and Shi A'er, all from Suzhou, and took them to the Gordon Road Police Station for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. The police station brought all the seized items to the court. The police station's lawyer, Jiang Baolian, presented the case, stating that after detaining the four defendants, they confessed that they had sold red pills to the Chang'an Lane No. 267 brothel on the French Concession's vegetable market road, and that the mastermind, Jiang Peisheng, lived at No. 24 Hekang Lane, Nine Acres. The police station then joined forces with French Concession detectives to investigate, but Jiang had already fled upon hearing the news and was not arrested. Only a woman, Zhang Zhou, her son Zhang A'yue, and the second landlord, Chen A'ming, were detained in Chang'an Lane and taken to the French Concession Police Station. They were sent to the Second Special District Court for questioning yesterday morning. The police station still needs to investigate the four defendants and requested permission to postpone the trial. Judge Wu Tingqi briefly questioned the four defendants and ordered them to be detained for another seven days.

More Rare Treasures Are Being Shipped to the Chicago World's Fair

Two Pairs of Jadeite Masterpieces

Now, it has been learned that a certain jeweler in this city, in view of the upcoming continuation of the fair in Chicago in June this year, plans to ship two pairs of jadeite masterpieces, worth a fortune and the result of ten years of painstaking research, to participate in the exhibition. One is a pair of flower baskets with chains, containing rare flowers, insects, and plants, named "Golden Jade Filling the Hall." They are truly top-grade yellow jade. As for their exquisite style and delicate carvings, they are breathtaking. The Chengdu Road Police Station Is Established

The Public Works Department of the Shanghai Municipal Council, considering that the western district is vast and that commerce in the area has flourished in recent years, with residents gradually increasing, has decided that security matters should be given extra attention. The police force of the existing police stations is already sufficient to bear the responsibility of protection, but the jurisdiction of the Xinzha Police Station seems to be too broad. To prevent any potential gaps in coverage, a new police station has been built on Chengdu Road in a suitable location, forming a staggered relationship with the Xinzha Police Station. If any incidents such as theft occur in the Xinzha area, the two police stations can jointly respond more quickly and effectively. The construction of this new building began not long ago and has now been completed. The interior layout is also modern. Because it is located on Chengdu Road, it is named the Chengdu Road Police Station after the location. All Chinese and Western staff, from the police chief to the constables, have been selected and appointed by the Chief of the Police Department. It officially started work yesterday. It is heard that the jurisdiction is divided from the Xinzha Police Station and the Gordon Road Police Station.

The Yong'an Company Robbery Case: Ten Criminals, Male and Female, Are Arrested in Western Shanghai. A Basket of Banknotes Was Hidden Under the Bed. Making a Fortune, Spreading the News, The Thugs Were All Watching.｜Rumors About How Wang Baokang Got the Stolen Goods｜

On the afternoon of December 6th last year, the Yong'an Company department store on Nanjing Road was robbed of 18,003 yuan in cash. The General Police Station, under the command of Chief Inspector Lu Liankui and other detectives, has successively arrested six robbers, including Yan Amao, Hu Songshan, Feng Zuowen, Pan Meimei, Lin Yunliang, and Lin Yuncai, and confiscated pistols and over 9,000 yuan of stolen money. This has been reported in this newspaper many times. Now, Lu Ying, the captain of the Criminal Investigation Team of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, stationed in the Western Shanghai area, along with Tang Bingxiang, the leader, and Gu Wentao, the inspector, and Song Chengfa, the sergeant of the Laborite Road branch of the Sixth District, have arrested another ten male and female criminals related to this case and recovered over 1,150 yuan in cash. The details are quite bizarre and interesting. The details are recorded below.

A Tip-Off from an Argument

On the night of the 4th of this month, Tang Bingxiang, the leader of the Criminal Investigation Team of the Sixth District of Western Shanghai, led various detectives, along with Inspector Gu Wentao and Sergeant Song Chengfa, to patrol Laborite Road. Suddenly, they saw four or five rickshaw pullers in a small porridge shop arguing with each other. Suddenly, one of them said, "Wang Baokang, Meng Guopei, Wang Jinkui, Zhou, etc. are all rich now." Leader Tang and others immediately went forward to inquire. It was claimed that Wang Baokang was one of the thieves who robbed the large sum of money from the Yong'an Company and is now hiding in Shudeli, Laborite Road. On the morning of the 5th, Leader Tang and others received a secret report that Meng Guopei, Wang Jinkui, Zhou Zhaoheng, and other criminals related to the robbery of the large sum of money from the Yong'an Company are now hiding in Shudeli.

Disguised as Vendors

Leader Tang and Inspector Gu reported the information to District Chief Tan, and immediately led detectives Sun Shucheng, Zhou Wenhai, Yang Zhongjin, Zhang Yuzhu, and Sergeant Song Chengfa, all disguised as vendors, to the address. They arrested Meng Guopei and Wang Qixian at No. 34 Shudeli, Laborite Road, Wang Jinkui at No. 49 Rongqingli, and Zhou Weitao, Zhou Weihong, and a woman, Zhou Wang, at No. 7 Fussenli, for a total of six people, and brought them back to the district. Over 100 yuan in stolen money was confiscated from the criminals.

A Basket of Banknotes

According to the woman Zhou, she is 51 years old, from Yancheng, and lives at No. 7 Fussenli. Wang Baokang is my common-law husband. He used to pull a rickshaw for a living and was very poor. Three weeks ago, I was sick and sleeping upstairs. My husband, Zhou Zhaoheng, suddenly saw a basket under Wang's bed, full of banknotes, all five-yuan and ten-yuan bills. Later, I questioned Wang about where he got so much money. Wang then said to my husband, "Don't say anything." Zhang Wang then gave my husband 1,000 yuan. Later, my husband counted the banknotes and there were only 910 yuan. Two days later, Meng Guopei and Wang Jinkui extorted 200 yuan by impersonating detectives. When a nephew died, over 200 yuan was used. Over 100 yuan was used to pay off debts. There are still over 400 yuan left, all with my husband. He has now fled to the French Concession. I really don't know where he is. Zhou Weihong is my eldest son, and Zhou Weitao is my second son. I also really don't know where Wang Baokang is.

Writing Letters to Collect Gambling Debts

According to Wang Qixian, he is 26 years old, from Shandong, and lives at No. 7 Shudeli. He works in a burlap bag factory for a living. Three weeks ago, my foster mother Zhou Wang said to me, "Wang Baokang is rich now. Why don't you go and collect the money he owes you?" After getting this news, because I lost to Wang Baokang at cards last month after work at the burlap bag factory, as a result, Wang owed me 320 jiao of small money, so I invited Wang Jinkui and Meng Guopei to go with me to collect the money from Wang Baokang. Wang said, "My foster father, Zhou Zhaoheng, is unreasonable. I already gave him 1,000 yuan, and he still took 500 yuan from my basket." At the time, Wang Baokang only gave me 40 yuan, which is true.

Extorting Money Again

According to Wang Jinkui, he is 40 years old, from Shandong, and lives at No. 7 Fussenli. Three weeks ago, Meng Guopei invited me to meet Wang Baokang at the Zhongtianfu Tea Garden on Laborite Road. Meng then impersonated a detective from the headquarters and said to Wang, "You are rich now. Be sensible, or I will arrest you and take you to court." After repeated entanglement, Wang gave 400 yuan. Later, they went to Zhou Zhaoheng's place and repeatedly threatened Zhou, and got another 180 yuan, for a total of 580 yuan. Meng took 150 yuan, Wang Qixian took 120 yuan, and I got 310 yuan. According to Zhou Weihong, 20 years old, and Zhou Weitao, 15 years old, both work in a burlap bag factory, Zhou Wang is their mother, and they don't know anything else. The detectives confiscated over 70 yuan in stolen money from the criminals.

Stolen Money in the Cellar

Soon after, a confidential informant reported that Wang Baokang was hiding the large sum of money at No. 20 Tianfunong, Tanzawan, Zhabei, at the place of his aunt, Wang Yang. After receiving the report, Leader Tang immediately led the original team of detectives and police officers from the Fourth District to the address. However, Wang had already fled upon hearing the news. Wang Yang, a suspect, and Zhang Shukui, a suspect, were arrested on the spot, and 480 yuan in original stolen money was unearthed from the cellar under the bed and brought back to the district. According to the woman, she is 40 years old. The money was sent to me by my nephew Wang Baokang. He left for Jiangbei the day before yesterday. I really don't know where the money came from. According to Zhang Shukui, he is 37 years old and used to be a factory worker. I was playing at his house and was arrested.

Arresting People in Shanyang County

After getting the confession, District Chief Tan of the Sixth District ordered Leader Tang to supervise the detectives and take Wang Yang and Zhang Shukui to Shanyang County, Jiangbei, on the 7th of this month, with a document, and work with the county to secretly go to Wang's house in Xujiazhuang in the countryside. However, Wang Baokang had already fled upon hearing the news. Wang's wife, Li, was arrested. According to Li, she is 20 years old. Baokang is my husband. On the evening of the 25th day of the tenth lunar month, I returned home from working at the Shanghai yarn factory. I heard people say that my husband was rich. I searched everywhere without success, and I became anxious and sick. My uncle sent me back to my hometown, but I couldn't find him. I only heard my uncle, Lu Wenbo, say that my husband had been there a few days ago and deposited 600 yuan with him. So I really don't know where my husband is.

Banknotes in the Mud Wall

The detectives then took Li to the flat in Lujiazhuang in the county and arrested Lu Yang, Lu Wenbo's wife. 600 yuan in cash was found in the mud wall, but Lu Wenbo had also escaped without a trace. Both women and the stolen money were taken back to the district. After District Chief Tan interrogated them separately, he ordered them to be sent to the General Bureau for questioning.

The Reason for Getting Rich

According to general rickshaw pullers, Wang Baokang got the large sum of money because when Yong'an was robbed, he happened to be parked there. A thief carrying the money fled and sat in his car and took it to the door of a foreign house (because he couldn't carry much in both hands). The patrolmen drove them away with sticks along the way. Wang then took this opportunity to escape back. When he arrived halfway, a rickshaw puller asked what was in his car. Wang said it was tin foil.

Apprentice of Tailor Shop Dies Tragically, Stealing Suspected and Scolded to Death, Injury Found Behind the Head of the Deceased

｜The Cause of Death Still Needs Autopsy｜

Shi Shaoxing, a 17-year-old apprentice from Haimen at the Xufutai Western Clothing Tailor Shop, No. 325 Fushoufang, Dalianwan Road, was usually very diligent in his work and of good character. However, he was recently suspected of theft and was severely scolded by Xu Chen, the shop owner's wife. From then on, he groaned in bed. The shop owner sent him to the hospital, but it was already incurable. He died. The police reported the investigation and took the body to the autopsy office. The First Special District Court's Prosecutor Guo found a wound on the back of the deceased's head after the autopsy, but because Xu Chen denied beating him, further investigation is needed. The woman was temporarily detained, and the police were ordered to investigate and verify the situation. This has been reported in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei, accompanied by forensic doctor and clerk, drove to the autopsy office on Fielun Road and ordered the gathering of a group of witnesses to continue the investigation. According to the report from the detectives of the Yulin Road Police Station, when the body of the deceased was taken out of the mortuary of the Sacred Heart Hospital, there was no injury behind his head. However, according to the report of forensic doctor Wei Ligong, the injury to the deceased was indeed sustained before death, and the wound was stabbed with something like scissors. If it were an injury after death, there would not be so much blood. Prosecutor Guo believed that the treatment of apprentices in old-fashioned shops was not civilized, which was a common practice and could not be denied. If an apprentice made a mistake, scolding and beating was even more common. Shi Shaoxing was found to have silver dollars in his shoes by the shop owner's wife, so he could not avoid being punished. He then questioned Xu Chen again and again, but she repeatedly denied beating him. The police investigation did not match the forensic examination, so the cause of death could not be completely clarified. It was then decided to send the injured part of the deceased to the Public Works Department's Hygiene Department for examination to determine whether the injury was sustained before or after death, so as to avoid wrongful conviction and value human life. The body was then released to the deceased's uncle, Shi Qixiang, who made a guarantee to take it away for burial. It is now known that Shi Qixiang believes that the forensic report is indeed true. His nephew, Shi Shaoxing, must have been injured by the shop owner's wife with sharp tailoring scissors and died. There is no doubt. Therefore, he has entrusted lawyer Wu Peng to handle the legal procedures against the shop owner couple yesterday.

The Taihu Water Conservancy Association Plans to Dredge the Wusong River

Requests Allocation of Cotton and Wheat Loans for Handling

The Taihu Basin Water Conservancy Commission believes that the Wusong River is a major drainage channel downstream of Taihu Lake, a major waterway between Shanghai and Suzhou and Changzhou, and that traffic is frequent. More than eight million acres of farmland in the counties along the river rely on it for irrigation. Its close relationship with the development of Shanghai's industry and commerce is even more important and needless to say. Since the Republic of China, it has not been dredged, the canal is blocked, and both agriculture and commerce are suffering. The commission, which is responsible for governing the Taihu Basin, has witnessed the difficult times and has prepared dredging plans and repeatedly requested funds to start construction. However, due to the empty treasury, it has not been implemented. Later, in April 1930, the Construction Committee invited various organizations to discuss the project plan and budget, which had been largely determined. However, due to the fundraising problem, it was not resolved and could not be realized. Now, the commission believes that the American cotton and wheat loans are specifically for rural use, and water conservancy construction is the top priority for rural revitalization. Moreover, the National Economic Commission has designated a part of the previous loan for water conservancy construction. The commission should prepare a dredging plan for the Wusong River and a budget, based on the original plan and taking into account the opinions of all parties. The commission has submitted it to the Ministry of Interior for forwarding to the government as soon as possible to allocate funds for construction.

The Commercial Press and Other Companies Have Established Safety Subcommittees

Labor-Management Cooperation to Promote Safety and Health

The Industrial Safety Association has recently been working hard on the safety work of its member factories. It has already passed the regulations on the organization of subcommittees in each factory at the last board meeting and has sent letters to each factory to actively prepare for the establishment of subcommittees to promote safety work in each factory. The organizational principle of the subcommittees focuses on cooperation between the factory and the labor union to jointly promote all safety and health work. In the past month, the Commercial Press Home Industry Society has established a safety subcommittee. The Zhonghua Book Company is scheduled to hold its inaugural meeting at the factory at 3:00 p.m. today (the 17th). It is heard that other member factories of the association, such as Gongqin Iron Factory, Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory, Tianchu Ajinomoto Factory, Zhenxing Textile Factory, Nanhua Rubber Factory, Hongxing Weaving Factory, Yihe Rubber Factory, and Dachina Welfare Rubber Factory, are actively preparing. Now, the association's regulations on the organization of subcommittees in each factory are as follows: (1) All member factories of the association may organize subcommittees in each factory to facilitate safety work. (2) The name of the subcommittee shall be the Industrial Safety Association ○○○ Factory Subcommittee (hereinafter referred to as the subcommittee). (3) The address of the subcommittee shall be located in each factory. (4) The organizational system of the subcommittee (diagram omitted). (5) The director or manager of each factory shall be the ex officio chairman of the subcommittee and shall be responsible for all matters of the subcommittee. (6) For the convenience of the subcommittee, the chairman shall select one or more instructors from among the factory staff to handle all matters under the chairman's order. (7) The original personnel department or other departments managing workers in each factory shall assist the instructors in promoting all safety work of the subcommittee. (8) The chairman may appoint the foremen or leaders of each workshop as safety officers of each workshop. If there is no foreman or leader, they may be selected from among the workers in each workshop. (When carrying out cleaning work, the safety officer may be renamed as a cleaning officer.) The safety officer shall lead the workers in each workshop to implement safety work. (9) The subcommittee shall establish a committee to discuss safety work plans and study safety and health facilities and improvements. (10) The members of the committee shall be instructors and safety officers. The factory director or manager shall be the chairman of the meeting. If there is a vacancy, the instructor shall act as the chairman. (11) The committee shall implement all safety work plans decided by the association (the association), study the implementation steps, and proceed on schedule. (12) All cases decided by the committee shall be implemented by the chairman. (13) The committee shall hold a regular meeting on the 5th of each month. If necessary, the chairman may convene an ad hoc meeting. (14) The association stipulates that the 10th of each month is Safety Day. On this day, each subcommittee shall conduct a factory-wide inspection by the chairman in conjunction with the instructor. If the above date falls on a rest day, it shall be postponed by one day. (15) When each subcommittee is established, it shall first report by letter, and then the association shall send someone to attend. (16) The bylaws of the subcommittee shall be determined by each factory and sent to the association for reference. (17) If there are any matters not covered in these regulations, the board of directors may amend them at any time. (18) These regulations shall come into force from the date of their approval by the board of directors.

Request for United Efforts to Eliminate Unlicensed Seafarers

The China Marine Engineering Association sent a letter to the China Merchant Marine Captains Association, stating: Regarding the current regulations of the Ministry of Transportation, those crew members in the navigation and engineering departments who have not obtained licenses but have applied to the Ministry for examination within the specified time may be temporarily allowed to work. However, for others, as of November 30th of last year, the relevant maritime authorities should earnestly eliminate them and prohibit them from working in order to uphold the law. It has now been found that on various ships in Shanghai, many officers in the navigation and engineering departments have neither obtained certificates nor applied for examination, and the Shanghai Maritime Bureau has not complied with the order to eliminate them. Our association has repeatedly negotiated, but to no avail. Their intentions are difficult to understand. Currently, there are a significant number of licensed seafarers who are unemployed. If the bureau were truly diligent and devoted to public service, how could they be so biased? Now, for the sake of upholding the dignity of the law, our association proposes that the navigation and engineering departments cooperate and requests your association to send representatives to negotiate with the bureau on an agreed date and argue based on reason. As this matter concerns the development of maritime administration, we hereby send this letter, hoping that you will investigate and inform us of the names of the representatives and the date of negotiation as soon as possible and actively proceed with the matter.

The Shanghai Haining Road Gaoshou Chong Bingxun Chinese Shorthand School recently printed a book entitled "Bingxun Shorthand Primer," which was published yesterday. It is simple, easy to learn, convenient, and accurate. One can learn on one's own without a teacher. Those who are illiterate can become literate, read books and newspapers after learning. Those who are literate can write faster after reading. It is truly a great contribution to Chinese culture. The book was written by Mr. Yang in memory of his uncle, Yang Chiqing, and costs only forty cents per copy. Family Industry Association Organizes Invincible Broadcasting Station Precursor

The Shanghai Family Industry Association recently cooperated with the Lishudetang Broadcasting Radio Station to have the association take over all the hours from 6:00 PM to 12:00 AM daily as the Invincible Broadcasting Station, dedicated to promoting art and advocating Mandarin. The rest of the time is used for advertising by the Shudetang Advertising Department, which officially opened on the 15th of this month. At 12:00 noon on that day, a test broadcast was first conducted, broadcasting the Party Song and the Will, and other ceremonial programs. Then, the founder of the station, Mr. Li Ruijiu, gave a speech, saying, "Since the early days of the Shanghai broadcasting industry in 1927, our station began to use a 15-watt transmitter to broadcast. Gradually, we increased the power. Today, our station has a maximum power of 400 watts. Recently, we have received letters from Guangdong, Guangxi, Hunan, Hubei, Hebei, Shandong, Henan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Anhui, all stating that our station's test broadcasts in the past ten days have been successful, with the clarity and loudness of the sound no less than that of the Central Station. Our station has been research-oriented for several years since its establishment and does not engage in business. However, our station seeks further development and expansion. Six months later, a transmitter ten times larger than today's will be installed. We have now received the official license No. 24 from the Ministry of Transportation. However, the construction cost required to build a great radio station is huge, and the recurring expenses are even greater. Although our station has never been in business, we have to slightly collect advertisements to subsidize it. This is the origin of our station's establishment of an advertising department." The Invincible Broadcasting Station is scheduled to officially open on the 20th of this month. From 9:00 PM to 12:00 AM that afternoon, famous figures from Shanghai will be invited to broadcast Peking Opera to add to the fun. It is expected that the beautiful songs and melodies, and the sounds of stringed instruments will create a grand scene at that time.

Four Banks' Reserve Depot Issues Reserve Report

211th Time

The Four Banks' Reserve Depot is jointly established by the Yanyeh, Jincheng, Zhongnan, and Continental Banks, specializing in the issuance of banknotes of the Zhongnan Bank. According to the depot's issuance regulations, banknotes are issued with full reserves, with cash reserves accounting for at least 60% and security reserves accounting for at most 40%. It is announced publicly once a week, and reviewed by the reviewers and accountants of the four banks. The 211th announcement of the Shanghai Reserve Depot on January 13, 1934, is transcribed as follows: Total banknote command amount: 27,899,837 yuan. Total reserve fund: 27,899,837 yuan, including cash reserve: 21,935,137 yuan, and security reserve: 5,964,700 yuan.

Yong An Tang Asks for Prohibition of "Gai Pai" Pharmacies

The Social Bureau Has Ordered Rectification of Names

Tiger Balm Yong An Tang, located on Ningbo Road in this city, found that someone had opened a Yong An Pharmacy nearby. They sent a petition to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau, stating that the Yong An Pharmacy was fraudulently registering a trade name and requesting the Bureau to prohibit its use. The petition stated that Yong An Tang was originally established in Singapore, and a branch was established in Shanghai in the sixteenth year of the Republic [1927]. The trademark and trade name were registered according to law, with trademark registration number 18273 and trade name registration number 340, both recorded in the Ministry of Industry and the Trademark Bureau. However, it has now been discovered that a Yong An Pharmacy has been established at No. 437 Guangxi Road, near Yong An Tang. Upon investigation, it is believed that according to Article 19 of the General Rules for Merchants (omission), the fraudulent use of the Yong An trade name is a clear case of unfair competition. Furthermore, according to the *Da Wan Bao* of December 5, the pharmacy was even found to be sharing profits with Dr. Li Jianfeng, selling drugs at high prices. The reports in the newspapers at the time led social figures to mistakenly believe that Yong An Tang was responsible, and many people called to inquire. Therefore, because of the fraudulent use of the Yong An name, Yong An Tang's reputation was damaged. It is urgent to prohibit this. Yong An Tang specifically submitted this information, along with a copy of the December 5 newspaper, requesting the Bureau to investigate and prohibit the pharmacy from using the Yong An trade name to prevent deception and avoid losses, for the sake of public convenience. The Social Bureau's reply is as follows: the submission and newspaper have been noted. The pharmacy has been ordered to change its trade name and report it for filing. You are hereby informed. This is the reply, with the newspaper kept on file. Director Wu Xingya.

Letters to the Editor

To the Editor: Having read the news section of your newspaper on the 16th of this month, there is a "Traffic Department Zhenru Power Plant Established" news item and the record is slightly inaccurate. Our radio station, in view of the fact that during the January 28 Shanghai War, the power poles and lines of the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company were often broken by artillery shells, causing frequent obstacles to the station’s reporting operations, a power plant has been approved to be built within the Zhenru reporting station. It can generate electricity by itself in case of a power outage in the city. The nature is only for standby. At ordinary times, the Zhabei company’s electricity is still used. Deeply afraid of causing misunderstanding, I hereby send a letter to your newspaper and request that it be included in the "Letters to the Editor" section for correction. Sincerely, Editor-in-Chief, *Shen Bao*, Traffic Department International Radio Station, January 16.

To the Editor: According to Xu Fusheng, the manager of the Zhongxin Weaving Factory, the victim in question, our factory was unfortunately and unexpectedly burned down by a reckless cook at about 6:00 PM on the 13th of this month, with all the factory's inventory, property, and more than 100 looms being reduced to ashes, resulting in a very heavy loss. However, upon reading the newspaper report on the fire at our place, the wording was inconsistent with the facts. Our factory has a wealthy capital and sufficient inventory. The burnt machine cargo can be tested for embers. The reports are enough to harm the factory's reputation. Lawyer is entrusted on behalf of the dispatch, requesting the newspaper to make corrections immediately, to emphasize the point of view. In light of this, I will respond on behalf. Please check and grant corrections. Sincerely, Editor-in-Chief of *Shen Bao*, lawyer Zhang Ji, January 16.
